SENTIENT SPECIES:
Four-Armed Robots with Five-fold Symmetry: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have four arms. They have five-fold symmetry. They are cautious and believe in the survival of the fittest. They were created by the Empire of Flying Blue Dwarfoids on Wotan II as servants in 1295.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -1 CON: -2 INT: 1 CHA: 2
Flying Blue Dwarfoids: Fond of drink and industry - especially building strange contraptions. They have blue skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They can fly. They are cautious and always willing to listen. They developed from Immortal Blue Dwarfoids in 1266.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -1 CON: 1 INT: 0 CHA: -1

CIVILISATIONS:
THE SECOND REPUBLIC OF ROBOTS AND DWARFOIDS:
A well-established, fantastically wealthy Republic of 14 planets, with 65 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
41 billion Four-Armed Robots with Five-fold Symmetry.
24 billion Flying Blue Dwarfoids.

	Their Stats are: STR: -2 DEX: 1 CON: 2 INT: 0 CHA: -2

0:
IN THE BEGINNING, ALL WAS DARK.
THEN, PLANETS BEGAN TO FORM:
Buliw I, Dylox V, Filar II, Cukiv I, Sativex III, Gynou III, Aykop I, Atria I, Kalamis I, Wotan II, Bykop I, Orra V, Chroma III, Euniw VI, Fymos V, Autorog VI

Sentient Amorphous Dwarfoids arise on Orra V.
44:
Vast empty plains form on Euniw VI.
46:

The star of Bykop I goes nova, scraping the planet clean of all life!
47:

The giant spaceborne white crystal leaves the orbit of Buliw I and heads back into deep space.

Sentient Amorphous Koboldoids arise on Wotan II.

53:

The Amorphous Dwarfoids on Orra V achieve spaceflight and organise as a Republic, the Republic of Amorphous Dwarfoids.
